$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / Functions1

::Functions Level 1 #000::
Given the following function definition:
<pre>void Switch(int& a, int& b, int& c)
\{
	a = a * b + c;
\}
</pre>
What value is printed after the following statments?
<pre>int dogs = 4;
int bar = 5;
int numbers = 3;
Switch(dogs, bar, numbers);
cout << dogs << endl;</pre>
	{
	=23
	~4
	~22
	~5
	~32
	}

::Functions Level 1 #001::
Given the following function definition:
<pre>void Absolute(int& a, int& b, int& c)
\{
	b = a * b + c;
\}
</pre>
What value is printed after the following statments?
<pre>int dogs = 4;
int list = 5;
int item = 4;
Absolute(dogs, list, item);
cout << list << endl;</pre>
	{
	=24
	~5
	~27
	~4
	~36
	}

::Functions Level 1 #002::
Given the following function definition:
<pre>void Make(int a, int b, int& c)
\{
	a = a * b / c;
\}
</pre>
What value is printed after the following statments?
<pre>int item = 4;
int foo = 4;
int marks = 5;
Make(item, foo, marks);
cout << item << endl;</pre>
	{
	=4
	~0
	~3
	~7.5
	~1.5
	}

::Functions Level 1 #003::
Given the following function definition:
<pre>void Make(int& a, int& b, int c)
\{
	c = a - b / c;
\}
</pre>
What value is printed after the following statments?
<pre>int item = 2;

Make(item, marks, bar);
cout << bar << endl;</pre>
	{
	=4
	~4.5
	~0
	~2
	~-1
	}

<pre>void BinarySort(int a, int& b, int& c)
\{
	c = a - b / c;
\}
</pre>
What value is printed after the following statments?
<pre>int standings = 4;
int numbers = 2;
int item = 3;
BinarySort(standings, numbers, item);
cout << item << endl;</pre>
	{
	=4
	~3
	~0
	~5
	~-3
	}

<pre>void Find(int a, int b, int& c)
\{
	c = a % b + c;
\}
</pre>
What value is printed after the following statments?
<pre>int dogs = 2;
int foo = 4;
int item = 5;
Find(dogs, foo, item);
cout << item << endl;</pre>
	{
	=7
	~5
	~5.5
	~2
	~1
	}
